\section*{Нахождение 6-й производной}
\subsection*{Найдём 1-ю производную}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(10.000) = 0.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(\ln10.000) = \frac{0.000}{10.000}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(-\ln10.000) = -\frac{0.000}{10.000}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(10.000) = 0.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(x) = 1.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(5.000) = 0.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}((x+5.000)) = 0.000+1.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(\sin(x+5.000)) = 0.000+1.000*\cosx+5.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(\sin(x+5.000)*10.000) = 0.000+1.000*\cosx+5.000*10.000+0.000*\sinx+5.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}((-\ln10.000+\sin(x+5.000)*10.000)) = 0.000+1.000*\cosx+5.000*10.000+0.000*\sinx+5.000+-\frac{0.000}{10.000}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(3.000) = 0.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(10.000^{3.000}) = 0.000*\ln10.000*10.000^{3.000}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(10.000^{3.000}*(-\ln10.000+\sin(x+5.000)*10.000)) = 0.000*\ln10.000*10.000^{3.000}*-\ln10.000+\sinx+5.000*10.000+0.000+1.000*\cosx+5.000*10.000+0.000*\sinx+5.000+-\frac{0.000}{10.000}*10.000^{3.000}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(x) = 1.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(x) = 1.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(x^{x}) = x^{x}*1.000*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(10.000^{3.000}*(-\ln10.000+\sin(x+5.000)*10.000)+x^{x}) = x^{x}*1.000*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}+0.000*\ln10.000*10.000^{3.000}*-\ln10.000+\sinx+5.000*10.000+0.000+1.000*\cosx+5.000*10.000+0.000*\sinx+5.000+-\frac{0.000}{10.000}*10.000^{3.000}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(gd) = 0.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(s) = 0.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(gd^{s}) = gd^{s}*0.000*\lngd+s*\frac{0.000}{gd}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(r) = 0.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(r*gd^{s}) = 0.000*gd^{s}+gd^{s}*0.000*\lngd+s*\frac{0.000}{gd}*r
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(10.000^{3.000}*(-\ln10.000+\sin(x+5.000)*10.000)+x^{x}+r*gd^{s}) = 0.000*gd^{s}+gd^{s}*0.000*\lngd+s*\frac{0.000}{gd}*r+x^{x}*1.000*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}+0.000*\ln10.000*10.000^{3.000}*-\ln10.000+\sinx+5.000*10.000+0.000+1.000*\cosx+5.000*10.000+0.000*\sinx+5.000+-\frac{0.000}{10.000}*10.000^{3.000}
\end{equation}
\subsection*{Найдём 2-ю производную}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(x) = 1.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(\lnx) = \frac{1.000}{x}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(x) = 1.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(1.000) = 0.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(\frac{1.000}{x}) = \frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(x) = 1.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(x*\frac{1.000}{x}) = 1.000*\frac{1.000}{x}+\frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}*x
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}((\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x})) = 1.000*\frac{1.000}{x}+\frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}*x+\frac{1.000}{x}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(x) = 1.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(x) = 1.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(x^{x}) = x^{x}*1.000*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(x^{x}*(\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x})) = x^{x}*1.000*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}+1.000*\frac{1.000}{x}+\frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}*x+\frac{1.000}{x}*x^{x}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(1000.000) = 0.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(10.000) = 0.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(x) = 1.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(5.000) = 0.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}((x+5.000)) = 0.000+1.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(\cos(x+5.000)) = 0.000+1.000*-1.000*\sinx+5.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(\cos(x+5.000)*10.000) = 0.000+1.000*-1.000*\sinx+5.000*10.000+0.000*\cosx+5.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(\cos(x+5.000)*10.000*1000.000) = 0.000+1.000*-1.000*\sinx+5.000*10.000+0.000*\cosx+5.000*1000.000+0.000*\cosx+5.000*10.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(x^{x}*(\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x})+\cos(x+5.000)*10.000*1000.000) = 0.000+1.000*-1.000*\sinx+5.000*10.000+0.000*\cosx+5.000*1000.000+0.000*\cosx+5.000*10.000+x^{x}*1.000*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}+1.000*\frac{1.000}{x}+\frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}*x+\frac{1.000}{x}*x^{x}
\end{equation}

\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(x^{x}*(\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x})*(\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x})) = x^{x}*1.000*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}+1.000*\frac{1.000}{x}+\frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}*x+\frac{1.000}{x}*x^{x}*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}+1.000*\frac{1.000}{x}+\frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}*x+\frac{1.000}{x}*x^{x}*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}

\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(\frac{1.000}{x}) = \frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}((\frac{1.000}{x}+\frac{1.000}{x})) = \frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}+\frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}((\frac{1.000}{x}+\frac{1.000}{x})*x^{x}) = \frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}+\frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}*x^{x}+x^{x}*1.000*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}*\frac{1.000}{x}+\frac{1.000}{x}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(x^{x}*(\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x})*(\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x})+(\frac{1.000}{x}+\frac{1.000}{x})*x^{x}) = \frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}+\frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}*x^{x}+x^{x}*1.000*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}*\frac{1.000}{x}+\frac{1.000}{x}+x^{x}*1.000*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}+1.000*\frac{1.000}{x}+\frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}*x+\frac{1.000}{x}*x^{x}*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}+1.000*\frac{1.000}{x}+\frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}*x+\frac{1.000}{x}*x^{x}*\lnx+x*\frac{1.000}{x}
\end{equation}

\end{equation}
\begin{equation}

\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(x) = 1.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(1.000) = 0.000
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}(\frac{1.000}{x}) = \frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
	 \frac{d}{dx}((\frac{1.000}{x}+\frac{1.000}{x})) = \frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}+\frac{0.000*x-1.000*1.000}{x^{2.000}}

\end{equation}
